Grand Prix Trial Winners at Grand Prix Lyon 2015
================================================



 Posted in [GRAND PRIX LYON 2015](/en/events/coverage/gplyo15)
 on October 31, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/henke_author.jpg)
By Tobi Henke











As is tradition, the Friday before this Grand Prix once again had hundreds of players enter into the infamous single-elimination Grand Prix Trials: their last chance to earn two byes for the weekend's main event, our first chance to get an impression of what it takes to succeed in *Battle for Zendikar* Sealed Deck.


So check out all these winning decklists!







#### Olivier Gheysen, Grand Prix Trial Winner


##### 




![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
